PyTorch (ë”¥ëŸ¬ë‹)

PyTorchëŠ” Meta(Facebook)ê°€ ê°œë°œí•œ ì˜¤í”ˆì†ŒìŠ¤ ë”¥ëŸ¬ë‹ í”„ë ˆì„ì›Œí¬ë¡œ, ë™ì  ê³„ì‚° ê·¸ë˜í”„(Define-by-Run) ë°©ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ì§ê´€ì ì¸ ë””ë²„ê¹…ê³¼ ìœ ì—°í•œ ëª¨ë¸ ì„¤ê³„ê°€ ê°€ëŠ¥í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. ì—°êµ¬ ì»¤ë®¤ë‹ˆí‹°ì—ì„œ ê°€ì¥ ë„ë¦¬ ì‚¬ìš©ë˜ë©°, TorchScript/ONNXë¥¼ í†µí•œ í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ ë°°í¬ë„ ì§€ì›í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì„¤ì¹˜: pip install torch torchvision torchaudio  |  CUDA: pytorch.orgì—ì„œ í”Œë«í¼ë³„ ëª…ë ¹ì–´ í™•ì¸  |  í™•ì¸: python -c "import torch; print(torch.__version__); print(torch.cuda.is_available())"

í…ì„œ(Tensor) ê¸°ë³¸ ì—°ì‚°

import torch import numpy as np # í…ì„œ ìƒì„± a = torch.tensor([[1, 2], [3, 4]], dtype=torch.float32) # ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸ì—ì„œ b = torch.zeros(3, 4) # ì˜í–‰ë ¬ c = torch.ones(2, 3) # 1í–‰ë ¬ d = torch.randn(3, 3) # í‘œì¤€ì •ê·œë¶„í¬ ë‚œìˆ˜ e = torch.eye(3) # ë‹¨ìœ„í–‰ë ¬ f = torch.arange(0, 10, 2) # [0, 2, 4, 6, 8] g = torch.linspace(0, 1, 5) # [0, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1] h = torch.empty(2, 3).uniform_(0, 1) # ê· ì¼ë¶„í¬ ë‚œìˆ˜ (in-place) # ê¸°ë³¸ ìˆ˜í•™ ì—°ì‚° (ìš”ì†Œë³„) x = a + a # torch.add(a, a) x = a * a # torch.mul(a, a) â€” ìš”ì†Œë³„ ê³± x = a @ a # torch.matmul(a, a) â€” í–‰ë ¬ ê³± x = a.sum() # ì „ì²´ í•© â†’ ìŠ¤ì¹¼ë¼ tensor(10.) x = a.mean(dim=0) # ì—´ í‰ê·  â†’ tensor([2., 3.]) x = a.max(dim=1) # í–‰ ìµœëŒ€ â†’ values, indices ë°˜í™˜ x = torch.clamp(a, 0, 3) # ê°’ ë²”ìœ„ ì œí•œ [0, 3] # Shape ì¡°ì‘ t = torch.randn(2, 3, 4) t.shape # torch.Size([2, 3, 4]) r = t.view(6, 4) # reshape (ì—°ì† ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ í•„ìš”) r = t.reshape(6, 4) # reshape (ìë™ ë³µì‚¬) r = t.view(-1) # í‰íƒ„í™” â†’ (24,) r = t.unsqueeze(0) # (2,3,4) â†’ (1,2,3,4) â€” ì°¨ì› ì¶”ê°€ r = r.squeeze(0) # (1,2,3,4) â†’ (2,3,4) â€” ì°¨ì› ì œê±° r = t.permute(2, 0, 1) # ì¶• ì¬ë°°ì—´ (2,3,4) â†’ (4,2,3) r = t.transpose(0, 1) # ë‘ ì¶• êµí™˜ (2,3,4) â†’ (3,2,4) # ê²°í•© & ë¶„í•  x = torch.cat([a, a], dim=0) # í–‰ ë°©í–¥ ê²°í•© (4,2) x = torch.stack([a, a], dim=0) # ìƒˆ ì°¨ì›ìœ¼ë¡œ ìŒ“ê¸° (2,2,2) chunks = t.chunk(3, dim=1) # dim=1 ê¸°ì¤€ 3ë“±ë¶„ # íƒ€ì… ë³€í™˜ & NumPy í˜¸í™˜ f = a.to(torch.float64) # float32 â†’ float64 f = a.int() # â†’ int32 (ë‹¨ì¶•í˜•) n = a.numpy() # í…ì„œ â†’ NumPy (CPU, ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ê³µìœ ) t = torch.from_numpy(n) # NumPy â†’ í…ì„œ (ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ê³µìœ ) t = a.clone().detach() # ë…ë¦½ ë³µì‚¬ë³¸ (ê·¸ë˜í”„ ë¶„ë¦¬)

Autograd (ìë™ ë¯¸ë¶„)

# requires_grad=True â†’ ì—°ì‚° ì¶”ì , ìë™ ë¯¸ë¶„ ê°€ëŠ¥ x = torch.tensor([2.0, 3.0], requires_grad=True) y = x ** 2 + 3 * x + 1 # y = xÂ² + 3x + 1 loss = y.sum() loss.backward() # ì—­ì „íŒŒ â€” ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ ê³„ì‚° print(x.grad) # dy/dx = 2x + 3 â†’ tensor([7., 9.]) # ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ ì œì–´ x.grad.zero_() # ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ ì´ˆê¸°í™” (ì¶•ì  ë°©ì§€) # ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ ì¶”ì  ë¹„í™œì„±í™” (ì¶”ë¡ /ì „ì²˜ë¦¬ ì‹œ) with torch.no_grad(): y = x * 2 # ì—°ì‚° ì¶”ì  ì•ˆ í•¨ â†’ ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ì ˆì•½ y = x.detach() # ê·¸ë˜í”„ì—ì„œ ë¶„ë¦¬ëœ ìƒˆ í…ì„œ # ê³ ì°¨ ë¯¸ë¶„ x = torch.tensor([1.0], requires_grad=True) y = x ** 3 grad1 = torch.autograd.grad(y, x, create_graph=True)[0] # 3xÂ² = 3 grad2 = torch.autograd.grad(grad1, x)[0] # 6x = 6

nn.Module ëª¨ë¸ êµ¬ì¶•

import torch.nn as nn # ê¸°ë³¸ ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜ class Net(nn.Module): def __init__(self, num_classes=10): super().__init__() self.fc1 = nn.Linear(784, 256) self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm1d(256) self.fc2 = nn.Linear(256, 128) self.dropout = nn.Dropout(0.3) self.fc3 = nn.Linear(128, num_classes) def forward(self, x): x = torch.relu(self.bn1(self.fc1(x))) x = torch.relu(self.fc2(x)) x = self.dropout(x) # training ëª¨ë“œì—ì„œë§Œ í™œì„±í™” return self.fc3(x) # ë¶„ë¥˜: CrossEntropyLossê°€ softmax í¬í•¨ model = Net(num_classes=10) print(model) # ëª¨ë¸ êµ¬ì¡° ì¶œë ¥ # íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° í™•ì¸ total = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters()) trainable = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters() if p.requires_grad) print(f"ì „ì²´: {total:,} / í•™ìŠµ ê°€ëŠ¥: {trainable:,}") # íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° ìˆœíšŒ for name, param in model.named_parameters(): print(f"{name}: {param.shape}")

nn.Sequential & ModuleList

# nn.Sequential â€” ë ˆì´ì–´ë¥¼ ìˆœì„œëŒ€ë¡œ ìŒ“ê¸° model = nn.Sequential( nn.Linear(784, 256), nn.ReLU(), nn.BatchNorm1d(256), nn.Dropout(0.3), nn.Linear(256, 128), nn.ReLU(), nn.Linear(128, 10) ) # OrderedDictë¡œ ì´ë¦„ ë¶€ì—¬ from collections import OrderedDict model = nn.Sequential(OrderedDict([ ("fc1", nn.Linear(784, 256)), ("relu1", nn.ReLU()), ("fc2", nn.Linear(256, 10)), ])) model.fc1 # ì´ë¦„ìœ¼ë¡œ ë ˆì´ì–´ ì ‘ê·¼ # nn.ModuleList â€” ë™ì  ë ˆì´ì–´ êµ¬ì„± class DynamicNet(nn.Module): def __init__(self, layers_sizes): super().__init__() self.layers = nn.ModuleList([ nn.Linear(in_f, out_f) for in_f, out_f in zip(layers_sizes[:-1], layers_sizes[1:]) ]) def forward(self, x): for layer in self.layers[:-1]: x = torch.relu(layer(x)) return self.layers[-1](x) # nn.ModuleDict â€” ì¡°ê±´ë¶€ ë ˆì´ì–´ ì„ íƒ class FlexibleNet(nn.Module): def __init__(self, activation="relu"): super().__init__() self.fc = nn.Linear(784, 10) self.activations = nn.ModuleDict({ "relu": nn.ReLU(), "gelu": nn.GELU(), "silu": nn.SiLU(), }) self.act = self.activations[activation]

ì”ì°¨ ì—°ê²° & ê³ ê¸‰ íŒ¨í„´

# ì”ì°¨ ë¸”ë¡ (ResNet ìŠ¤íƒ€ì¼) class ResidualBlock(nn.Module): def __init__(self, dim): super().__init__() self.block = nn.Sequential( nn.Linear(dim, dim), nn.BatchNorm1d(dim), nn.ReLU(), nn.Linear(dim, dim), nn.BatchNorm1d(dim), ) def forward(self, x): return torch.relu(self.block(x) + x) # ì”ì°¨ ì—°ê²° # ë‹¤ì¤‘ ì…ë ¥ ëª¨ë¸ class MultiInputModel(nn.Module): def __init__(self): super().__init__() self.text_branch = nn.Linear(100, 64) self.meta_branch = nn.Linear(5, 16) self.classifier = nn.Linear(80, 10) def forward(self, text, meta): t = torch.relu(self.text_branch(text)) m = torch.relu(self.meta_branch(meta)) merged = torch.cat([t, m], dim=1) # íŠ¹ì„± ê²°í•© return self.classifier(merged)

ì£¼ìš” ë ˆì´ì–´ ë¹„êµ

ë ˆì´ì–´ìš©ë„ì£¼ìš” íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°ì…ë ¥ shape
nn.Linearì™„ì „ì—°ê²° (MLP)in_features, out_features(batch, features)
nn.Conv2dì´ë¯¸ì§€ íŠ¹ì§• ì¶”ì¶œin_channels, out_channels, kernel_size(batch, C, H, W)
nn.MaxPool2dê³µê°„ ë‹¤ìš´ìƒ˜í”Œë§kernel_size, stride(batch, C, H, W)
nn.LSTMì‹œê³„ì—´/ìˆœì°¨ ë°ì´í„°input_size, hidden_size, num_layers(seq, batch, features)
nn.GRUê²½ëŸ‰ ìˆœí™˜ ë ˆì´ì–´input_size, hidden_size(seq, batch, features)
nn.Embeddingì •ìˆ˜â†’ë°€ì§‘ ë²¡í„°num_embeddings, embedding_dim(batch, seq_len) ì •ìˆ˜
nn.BatchNorm1d/2dí•™ìŠµ ì•ˆì •í™”, ê°€ì†num_features(batch, features) / (B,C,H,W)
nn.Dropoutê³¼ì í•© ë°©ì§€p (0~1)ì„ì˜
nn.LayerNormTransformer ì •ê·œí™”normalized_shapeì„ì˜
nn.MultiheadAttentionì–´í…ì…˜ ë©”ì»¤ë‹ˆì¦˜embed_dim, num_heads(seq, batch, embed_dim)
TensorFlow vs PyTorch ì±„ë„ ìˆœì„œ: TensorFlow/KerasëŠ” (batch, H, W, C) â€” channels-last, PyTorchëŠ” (batch, C, H, W) â€” channels-firstê°€ ê¸°ë³¸ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. PyTorchì—ì„œ .permute(0, 3, 1, 2)ë¡œ ë³€í™˜í•˜ì„¸ìš”.

ì†ì‹¤ í•¨ìˆ˜(Loss Function)

ì‘ì—…ì†ì‹¤ í•¨ìˆ˜ì¶œë ¥ í˜•íƒœë ˆì´ë¸” í˜•íƒœ
ë‹¤ì¤‘ ë¶„ë¥˜nn.CrossEntropyLoss()raw logits (N, C)ì •ìˆ˜ (N,)
ì´ì§„ ë¶„ë¥˜nn.BCEWithLogitsLoss()raw logits (N, 1)float 0/1 (N, 1)
ì´ì§„ ë¶„ë¥˜ (sigmoid í›„)nn.BCELoss()í™•ë¥  (N, 1)float 0/1 (N, 1)
íšŒê·€nn.MSELoss()(N, *)(N, *)
íšŒê·€ (ì´ìƒì¹˜ ê°•ê±´)nn.SmoothL1Loss()(N, *)(N, *)
íšŒê·€ (L1)nn.L1Loss()(N, *)(N, *)
ë‹¤ì¤‘ ë ˆì´ë¸”nn.BCEWithLogitsLoss()raw logits (N, C)multi-hot (N, C)
# CrossEntropyLossëŠ” ë‚´ë¶€ì— softmaxë¥¼ í¬í•¨ â€” ëª¨ë¸ ì¶œë ¥ì— softmax ì ìš©í•˜ì§€ ë§ ê²ƒ! criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss() logits = model(x) # raw logits, softmax ì ìš© ì•ˆ í•¨ loss = criterion(logits, labels) # labels: ì •ìˆ˜ í…ì„œ (LongTensor) # í´ë˜ìŠ¤ ë¶ˆê· í˜• ì²˜ë¦¬ weights = torch.tensor([1.0, 5.0, 1.0]) # í´ë˜ìŠ¤ë³„ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss(weight=weights.to(device)) # ì»¤ìŠ¤í…€ ì†ì‹¤ í•¨ìˆ˜ class FocalLoss(nn.Module): def __init__(self, alpha=1.0, gamma=2.0): super().__init__() self.alpha = alpha self.gamma = gamma def forward(self, inputs, targets): ce_loss = nn.functional.cross_entropy(inputs, targets, reduction="none") pt = torch.exp(-ce_loss) return (self.alpha * (1 - pt) ** self.gamma * ce_loss).mean()

ì˜µí‹°ë§ˆì´ì €(Optimizer) & ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¤„ëŸ¬

import torch.optim as optim # ì£¼ìš” ì˜µí‹°ë§ˆì´ì € optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.01, momentum=0.9, weight_decay=1e-4) optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=1e-3, weight_decay=1e-4) optim.AdamW(model.parameters(), lr=1e-3, weight_decay=1e-2) # ë¶„ë¦¬ëœ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ ê°ì‡  optim.RMSprop(model.parameters(), lr=1e-3) # íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° ê·¸ë£¹ë³„ í•™ìŠµë¥  ì„¤ì • optimizer = optim.Adam([ {"params": model.fc1.parameters(), "lr": 1e-4}, # ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ë ˆì´ì–´ (ë‚®ì€ lr) {"params": model.fc3.parameters(), "lr": 1e-3}, # ìƒˆ ë ˆì´ì–´ (ë†’ì€ lr) ], weight_decay=1e-4) # í•™ìŠµë¥  ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¤„ëŸ¬ scheduler = optim.lr_scheduler.StepLR(optimizer, step_size=10, gamma=0.1) # 10 ì—í¬í¬ë§ˆë‹¤ Ã—0.1 scheduler = optim.lr_scheduler.CosineAnnealingLR(optimizer, T_max=50) # ì½”ì‚¬ì¸ ê°ì‡  scheduler = optim.lr_scheduler.ReduceLROnPlateau( # ì •ì²´ ì‹œ ê°ì†Œ optimizer, mode="min", factor=0.5, patience=5 ) scheduler = optim.lr_scheduler.OneCycleLR( # 1-Cycle ì •ì±… optimizer, max_lr=0.01, total_steps=1000 ) # ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¤„ëŸ¬ ì‚¬ìš© (í•™ìŠµ ë£¨í”„ ë‚´ì—ì„œ) # scheduler.step() â€” ì—í¬í¬ ê¸°ë°˜ (StepLR, CosineAnnealing) # scheduler.step(val_loss) â€” ë©”íŠ¸ë¦­ ê¸°ë°˜ (ReduceLROnPlateau) # scheduler.step() â€” ë°°ì¹˜ ê¸°ë°˜ (OneCycleLR) â€” ë§¤ ë°°ì¹˜ í›„ í˜¸ì¶œ

í‘œì¤€ í•™ìŠµ ë£¨í”„

import torch import torch.nn as nn import torch.optim as optim device = torch.device("cuda" if torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu") model = Net().to(device) criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss() optimizer = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=1e-3) scheduler = optim.lr_scheduler.CosineAnnealingLR(optimizer, T_max=20) # í•™ìŠµ í•¨ìˆ˜ def train_one_epoch(model, loader, criterion, optimizer, device): model.train() # Dropout, BatchNorm í•™ìŠµ ëª¨ë“œ running_loss = 0.0 correct = 0 total = 0 for inputs, labels in loader: inputs, labels = inputs.to(device), labels.to(device) optimizer.zero_grad() # â‘  ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ ì´ˆê¸°í™” outputs = model(inputs) # â‘¡ ìˆœì „íŒŒ loss = criterion(outputs, labels) loss.backward() # â‘¢ ì—­ì „íŒŒ optimizer.step() # â‘£ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ ê°±ì‹  running_loss += loss.item() * inputs.size(0) _, predicted = outputs.max(1) total += labels.size(0) correct += predicted.eq(labels).sum().item() return running_loss / total, correct / total # ê²€ì¦ í•¨ìˆ˜ @torch.no_grad() # ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ ë¹„í™œì„±í™” def evaluate(model, loader, criterion, device): model.eval() # Dropout ë¹„í™œì„±í™”, BatchNorm ê³ ì • running_loss = 0.0 correct = 0 total = 0 for inputs, labels in loader: inputs, labels = inputs.to(device), labels.to(device) outputs = model(inputs) loss = criterion(outputs, labels) running_loss += loss.item() * inputs.size(0) _, predicted = outputs.max(1) total += labels.size(0) correct += predicted.eq(labels).sum().item() return running_loss / total, correct / total # í•™ìŠµ ë£¨í”„ (EarlyStopping í¬í•¨) best_val_loss = float("inf") patience_counter = 0 for epoch in range(100): train_loss, train_acc = train_one_epoch(model, train_loader, criterion, optimizer, device) val_loss, val_acc = evaluate(model, val_loader, criterion, device) scheduler.step() print(f"[{epoch+1:3d}] train_loss={train_loss:.4f} acc={train_acc:.4f} | val_loss={val_loss:.4f} acc={val_acc:.4f}") if val_loss < best_val_loss: best_val_loss = val_loss patience_counter = 0 torch.save(model.state_dict(), "best_model.pt") # ìµœì  ëª¨ë¸ ì €ì¥ else: patience_counter += 1 if patience_counter >= 10: print("Early stopping!") break model.load_state_dict(torch.load("best_model.pt")) # ìµœì  ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ ë³µì›

DataLoader & Dataset

from torch.utils.data import Dataset, DataLoader, TensorDataset, random_split # â‘  TensorDataset â€” NumPy/í…ì„œì—ì„œ ë°”ë¡œ ìƒì„± dataset = TensorDataset( torch.tensor(X_train, dtype=torch.float32), torch.tensor(y_train, dtype=torch.long) ) # â‘¡ ì»¤ìŠ¤í…€ Dataset class MyDataset(Dataset): def __init__(self, data, labels, transform=None): self.data = data self.labels = labels self.transform = transform def __len__(self): return len(self.data) def __getitem__(self, idx): sample = self.data[idx] label = self.labels[idx] if self.transform: sample = self.transform(sample) return sample, label # DataLoader â€” ë°°ì¹˜, ì…”í”Œ, ë³‘ë ¬ ë¡œë”© train_loader = DataLoader( dataset, batch_size=64, shuffle=True, # í•™ìŠµ ë°ì´í„° ì…”í”Œ num_workers=4, # ë³‘ë ¬ ë°ì´í„° ë¡œë”© í”„ë¡œì„¸ìŠ¤ pin_memory=True, # GPU ì „ì†¡ ê°€ì† (CUDA) drop_last=True, # ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ë¶ˆì™„ì „ ë°°ì¹˜ ì œê±° ) val_loader = DataLoader(dataset, batch_size=128, shuffle=False) # ë°ì´í„° ë¶„í•  train_set, val_set = random_split(dataset, [0.8, 0.2]) # ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ë°ì´í„°: torchvision transforms from torchvision import transforms, datasets transform_train = transforms.Compose([ transforms.RandomResizedCrop(224), transforms.RandomHorizontalFlip(), transforms.ColorJitter(brightness=0.2, contrast=0.2), transforms.ToTensor(), transforms.Normalize(mean=[0.485, 0.456, 0.406], std=[0.229, 0.224, 0.225]) ]) transform_val = transforms.Compose([ transforms.Resize(256), transforms.CenterCrop(224), transforms.ToTensor(), transforms.Normalize(mean=[0.485, 0.456, 0.406], std=[0.229, 0.224, 0.225]) ]) # ë‚´ì¥ ë°ì´í„°ì…‹ (CIFAR-10, MNIST, ImageNet ë“±) train_ds = datasets.CIFAR10("./data", train=True, download=True, transform=transform_train) train_loader = DataLoader(train_ds, batch_size=64, shuffle=True, num_workers=4) # ImageFolder â€” ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ êµ¬ì¡°ì—ì„œ ìë™ ë¡œë”© (data/train/cat/*.jpg, data/train/dog/*.jpg) train_ds = datasets.ImageFolder("data/train", transform=transform_train)

ëª¨ë¸ ì €ì¥ ë° ë¡œë“œ

# â‘  state_dict ì €ì¥/ë¡œë“œ (ê¶Œì¥ â€” ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ë§Œ, ì½”ë“œ ìœ ì§€) torch.save(model.state_dict(), "model_weights.pt") model = Net() # ëª¨ë¸ êµ¬ì¡° ì¬ìƒì„± í•„ìš” model.load_state_dict(torch.load("model_weights.pt", weights_only=True)) model.eval() # â‘¡ ì „ì²´ ëª¨ë¸ ì €ì¥ (êµ¬ì¡° + ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ â€” pickle ì˜ì¡´) torch.save(model, "full_model.pt") model = torch.load("full_model.pt", weights_only=False) # â‘¢ ì²´í¬í¬ì¸íŠ¸ ì €ì¥ (í•™ìŠµ ì¬ê°œìš©) torch.save({ "epoch": epoch, "model_state_dict": model.state_dict(), "optimizer_state_dict": optimizer.state_dict(), "scheduler_state_dict": scheduler.state_dict(), "best_val_loss": best_val_loss, }, "checkpoint.pt") # ì²´í¬í¬ì¸íŠ¸ ë³µì› ckpt = torch.load("checkpoint.pt", weights_only=False) model.load_state_dict(ckpt["model_state_dict"]) optimizer.load_state_dict(ckpt["optimizer_state_dict"]) scheduler.load_state_dict(ckpt["scheduler_state_dict"]) start_epoch = ckpt["epoch"] + 1 # â‘£ TorchScript ë³€í™˜ (C++/í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ ë°°í¬) scripted = torch.jit.script(model) # Python ì œì–´íë¦„ í¬í•¨ ê°€ëŠ¥ scripted.save("model_scripted.pt") traced = torch.jit.trace(model, torch.randn(1, 784)) # ì…ë ¥ ê¸°ë°˜ ì¶”ì  traced.save("model_traced.pt") loaded = torch.jit.load("model_scripted.pt") # â‘¤ ONNX ë³€í™˜ dummy = torch.randn(1, 784) torch.onnx.export(model, dummy, "model.onnx", input_names=["input"], output_names=["output"], dynamic_axes={"input": {0: "batch"}, "output": {0: "batch"}})

GPU & ë””ë°”ì´ìŠ¤ ê´€ë¦¬

# ë””ë°”ì´ìŠ¤ ì„¤ì • device = torch.device("cuda" if torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu") device = torch.device("cuda:0") # íŠ¹ì • GPU ì§€ì • # í…ì„œ/ëª¨ë¸ì„ ë””ë°”ì´ìŠ¤ë¡œ ì´ë™ x = x.to(device) # í…ì„œ ì´ë™ model = model.to(device) # ëª¨ë¸ ì´ë™ (íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° + ë²„í¼) # GPU ì •ë³´ í™•ì¸ torch.cuda.is_available() # GPU ì‚¬ìš© ê°€ëŠ¥ ì—¬ë¶€ torch.cuda.device_count() # GPU ê°œìˆ˜ torch.cuda.get_device_name(0) # GPU ì´ë¦„ torch.cuda.memory_allocated() # í˜„ì¬ ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ì‚¬ìš©ëŸ‰ torch.cuda.memory_reserved() # ì˜ˆì•½ëœ ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ torch.cuda.empty_cache() # ë¯¸ì‚¬ìš© ìºì‹œ í•´ì œ # í˜¼í•© ì •ë°€ë„ í•™ìŠµ (AMP) â€” ì†ë„ 2ë°°â†‘, ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ì ˆê° scaler = torch.amp.GradScaler() for inputs, labels in loader: inputs, labels = inputs.to(device), labels.to(device) optimizer.zero_grad() with torch.amp.autocast(device_type="cuda"): # float16 ìë™ ë³€í™˜ outputs = model(inputs) loss = criterion(outputs, labels) scaler.scale(loss).backward() # ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¼ë§ëœ ì—­ì „íŒŒ scaler.step(optimizer) # ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ ê°±ì‹  scaler.update() # ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¼ ì¡°ì • # ë©€í‹° GPU (DataParallel â€” ê°„ë‹¨í•˜ì§€ë§Œ ë¹„íš¨ìœ¨) if torch.cuda.device_count() > 1: model = nn.DataParallel(model) # ë°°ì¹˜ë¥¼ GPUì— ë¶„ë°° model = model.to(device) # ë©€í‹° GPU (DistributedDataParallel â€” ê¶Œì¥, ê³ ì„±ëŠ¥) # torchrun --nproc_per_node=4 train.py import torch.distributed as dist from torch.nn.parallel import DistributedDataParallel as DDP dist.init_process_group(backend="nccl") local_rank = int(os.environ["LOCAL_RANK"]) model = DDP(model.to(local_rank), device_ids=[local_rank])
ì£¼ì˜ì‚¬í•­: model.train()ê³¼ model.eval()ì„ í•™ìŠµ/ì¶”ë¡  ì „ì— ë°˜ë“œì‹œ í˜¸ì¶œí•˜ì„¸ìš” â€” Dropoutê³¼ BatchNormì˜ ë™ì‘ì´ ë‹¬ë¼ì§‘ë‹ˆë‹¤. CrossEntropyLossëŠ” softmaxë¥¼ ë‚´ì¥í•˜ë¯€ë¡œ ëª¨ë¸ ì¶œë ¥ì— softmaxë¥¼ ì¤‘ë³µ ì ìš©í•˜ë©´ ì•ˆ ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤. loss.backward() ì „ì— optimizer.zero_grad()ë¥¼ í˜¸ì¶œí•˜ì„¸ìš” â€” PyTorchëŠ” ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ë¥¼ ê¸°ë³¸ìœ¼ë¡œ ëˆ„ì í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì¶”ë¡  & ë°°í¬

# ì¶”ë¡  ëª¨ë“œ â€” ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ìµœì í™”, autograd ì™„ì „ ë¹„í™œì„±í™” model.eval() with torch.inference_mode(): # torch.no_grad()ë³´ë‹¤ ë¹ ë¦„ predictions = model(x.to(device)) probs = torch.softmax(predictions, dim=1) classes = probs.argmax(dim=1) # ë°°ì¹˜ ì¶”ë¡  (ëŒ€ëŸ‰ ë°ì´í„°) all_preds = [] model.eval() with torch.inference_mode(): for batch in test_loader: inputs = batch[0].to(device) preds = model(inputs).argmax(dim=1) all_preds.append(preds.cpu()) all_preds = torch.cat(all_preds) # torch.compile â€” PyTorch 2.0+ ìë™ ìµœì í™” (JIT ì»´íŒŒì¼) model = torch.compile(model) # ì²« ì‹¤í–‰ ì‹œ ì»´íŒŒì¼, ì´í›„ ê°€ì† model = torch.compile(model, mode="reduce-overhead") # ì˜¤ë²„í—¤ë“œ ìµœì†Œí™”

ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ í´ë¦¬í•‘ & ì •ê·œí™”

# ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ í´ë¦¬í•‘ â€” ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ í­ë°œ ë°©ì§€ (RNN, Transformer í•„ìˆ˜) loss.backward() torch.nn.utils.clip_grad_norm_(model.parameters(), max_norm=1.0) # L2 norm ê¸°ì¤€ torch.nn.utils.clip_grad_value_(model.parameters(), clip_value=0.5) # ì ˆëŒ€ê°’ ê¸°ì¤€ optimizer.step() # ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ ì´ˆê¸°í™” def init_weights(m): if isinstance(m, nn.Linear): nn.init.kaiming_normal_(m.weight, mode="fan_out", nonlinearity="relu") if m.bias is not None: nn.init.zeros_(m.bias) elif isinstance(m, nn.Conv2d): nn.init.kaiming_normal_(m.weight, mode="fan_out") model.apply(init_weights) # ëª¨ë“  í•˜ìœ„ ëª¨ë“ˆì— ì¬ê·€ ì ìš© # ë ˆì´ì–´ ë™ê²° (ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ) for param in model.fc1.parameters(): param.requires_grad = False # fc1 ë ˆì´ì–´ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ ê³ ì • # ë™ê²°ëœ íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° ì œì™¸í•œ ì˜µí‹°ë§ˆì´ì € optimizer = optim.Adam(filter(lambda p: p.requires_grad, model.parameters()), lr=1e-3)

PyTorch í•µì‹¬ ì •ë¦¬

ì‘ì—…API / ë©”ì„œë“œë¹„ê³ 
ëª¨ë¸ ì •ì˜nn.Module ìƒì†__init__ + forward
ê°„ë‹¨í•œ ëª¨ë¸nn.Sequentialì´ë¦„ ë¶€ì—¬ ì‹œ OrderedDict
í•™ìŠµ ëª¨ë“œmodel.train()Dropout/BN í™œì„±í™”
ì¶”ë¡  ëª¨ë“œmodel.eval() + inference_mode()ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ìµœì í™”
ì—­ì „íŒŒloss.backward()zero_grad â†’ forward â†’ backward â†’ step
ë°ì´í„° ë¡œë”©DataLoaderpin_memory=True (GPU)
ëª¨ë¸ ì €ì¥torch.save(state_dict)ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ë§Œ ì €ì¥ ê¶Œì¥
ì²´í¬í¬ì¸íŠ¸dictë¡œ epoch/optimizer í¬í•¨ ì €ì¥í•™ìŠµ ì¬ê°œìš©
í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ ë°°í¬torch.jit.script/traceTorchScript C++ ëŸ°íƒ€ì„
ì„±ëŠ¥ í–¥ìƒtorch.compile()PyTorch 2.0+ JIT ì»´íŒŒì¼
í˜¼í•© ì •ë°€ë„torch.amp.autocastGradScaler í•„ìˆ˜
ë©€í‹° GPUDistributedDataParalleltorchrunìœ¼ë¡œ ì‹¤í–‰
ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ í´ë¦¬í•‘clip_grad_norm_RNN/Transformer í•„ìˆ˜

CNN (í•©ì„±ê³± ì‹ ê²½ë§)

í•©ì„±ê³± ì‹ ê²½ë§(Convolutional Neural Network)ì€ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì¸ì‹, ê°ì²´ íƒì§€, ì„¸ê·¸ë©˜í…Œì´ì…˜ ë“± ì‹œê°ì  íŒ¨í„´ ì¸ì‹ì— ìµœì í™”ëœ ì•„í‚¤í…ì²˜ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. í•©ì„±ê³± ë ˆì´ì–´ê°€ ê³µê°„ì  íŠ¹ì§•ì„ ê³„ì¸µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì¶”ì¶œí•˜ê³ , í’€ë§ìœ¼ë¡œ ì°¨ì›ì„ ì¤„ì¸ ë’¤ ì™„ì „ì—°ê²°ì¸µì—ì„œ ë¶„ë¥˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

í•©ì„±ê³± ì—°ì‚° ì´í•´

# Conv2D í•µì‹¬ íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° ì´í•´ # # ì…ë ¥: (batch, H, W, C) â€” Keras / (batch, C, H, W) â€” PyTorch # # filters/out_channels : ì¶œë ¥ íŠ¹ì„±ë§µ ìˆ˜ (í•™ìŠµí•  í•„í„° ê°œìˆ˜) # kernel_size : í•„í„° í¬ê¸° (3Ã—3ì´ ê°€ì¥ ë³´í¸ì ) # strides : í•„í„° ì´ë™ ê°„ê²© (2ì´ë©´ ì¶œë ¥ í¬ê¸° ì ˆë°˜) # padding : "same" â†’ ì…ì¶œë ¥ í¬ê¸° ë™ì¼, "valid" â†’ íŒ¨ë”© ì—†ìŒ # # ì¶œë ¥ í¬ê¸° ê³„ì‚°: O = (I - K + 2P) / S + 1 # I=ì…ë ¥í¬ê¸°, K=ì»¤ë„í¬ê¸°, P=íŒ¨ë”©, S=ìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¼ì´ë“œ # ì˜ˆ: ì…ë ¥ 28Ã—28, kernel=3, padding=0, stride=1 â†’ 26Ã—26 # ì˜ˆ: ì…ë ¥ 28Ã—28, kernel=3, padding=1, stride=1 â†’ 28Ã—28 (same) # ì˜ˆ: ì…ë ¥ 28Ã—28, kernel=3, padding=0, stride=2 â†’ 13Ã—13

CNN â€” Keras êµ¬í˜„

from tensorflow import keras from tensorflow.keras import layers # ê¸°ë³¸ CNN (MNIST ë¶„ë¥˜) model = keras.Sequential([ # ë¸”ë¡ 1: í•©ì„±ê³± â†’ ì •ê·œí™” â†’ í™œì„±í™” â†’ í’€ë§ layers.Conv2D(32, (3, 3), padding="same", input_shape=(28, 28, 1)), layers.BatchNormalization(), layers.ReLU(), layers.MaxPooling2D((2, 2)), # 28Ã—28 â†’ 14Ã—14 # ë¸”ë¡ 2 layers.Conv2D(64, (3, 3), padding="same"), layers.BatchNormalization(), layers.ReLU(), layers.MaxPooling2D((2, 2)), # 14Ã—14 â†’ 7Ã—7 # ë¸”ë¡ 3 layers.Conv2D(128, (3, 3), padding="same"), layers.BatchNormalization(), layers.ReLU(), layers.GlobalAveragePooling2D(), # 7Ã—7Ã—128 â†’ 128 (Flatten ëŒ€ì‹  ê¶Œì¥) # ë¶„ë¥˜ í—¤ë“œ layers.Dropout(0.5), layers.Dense(10, activation="softmax") ]) model.compile(optimizer="adam", loss="sparse_categorical_crossentropy", metrics=["accuracy"]) # 1D í•©ì„±ê³± (í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸, ì‹œê³„ì—´) text_cnn = keras.Sequential([ layers.Embedding(10000, 128, input_length=200), layers.Conv1D(64, 5, activation="relu"), # 5-gram íŠ¹ì§• ì¶”ì¶œ layers.GlobalMaxPooling1D(), layers.Dense(1, activation="sigmoid") ])

CNN â€” PyTorch êµ¬í˜„

import torch import torch.nn as nn class CNN(nn.Module): def __init__(self, num_classes=10): super().__init__() self.features = nn.Sequential( # ë¸”ë¡ 1 nn.Conv2d(1, 32, kernel_size=3, padding=1), # (1,28,28)â†’(32,28,28) nn.BatchNorm2d(32), nn.ReLU(inplace=True), nn.MaxPool2d(2), # â†’(32,14,14) # ë¸”ë¡ 2 nn.Conv2d(32, 64, kernel_size=3, padding=1), # â†’(64,14,14) nn.BatchNorm2d(64), nn.ReLU(inplace=True), nn.MaxPool2d(2), # â†’(64,7,7) # ë¸”ë¡ 3 nn.Conv2d(64, 128, kernel_size=3, padding=1), nn.BatchNorm2d(128), nn.ReLU(inplace=True), nn.AdaptiveAvgPool2d((1, 1)), # â†’(128,1,1) ì–´ë–¤ ì…ë ¥ í¬ê¸°ë“  OK ) self.classifier = nn.Sequential( nn.Flatten(), nn.Dropout(0.5), nn.Linear(128, num_classes), ) def forward(self, x): x = self.features(x) return self.classifier(x) # Depthwise Separable Convolution (MobileNet ìŠ¤íƒ€ì¼ â€” ê²½ëŸ‰í™”) depthwise_sep = nn.Sequential( nn.Conv2d(64, 64, 3, padding=1, groups=64), # depthwise: ì±„ë„ë³„ ë…ë¦½ í•©ì„±ê³± nn.Conv2d(64, 128, 1), # pointwise: 1Ã—1 í•©ì„±ê³±ìœ¼ë¡œ ì±„ë„ ê²°í•© ) # Dilated (Atrous) Convolution â€” ìˆ˜ìš© ì˜ì—­ í™•ì¥ dilated = nn.Conv2d(64, 64, 3, padding=2, dilation=2) # 3Ã—3 í•„í„°ê°€ 5Ã—5 ì˜ì—­ ì»¤ë²„ # Transposed Convolution â€” ì—…ìƒ˜í”Œë§ (ì„¸ê·¸ë©˜í…Œì´ì…˜, GAN ìƒì„±ê¸°) upsample = nn.ConvTranspose2d(64, 32, kernel_size=4, stride=2, padding=1) # í¬ê¸° 2ë°°

ì£¼ìš” CNN ì•„í‚¤í…ì²˜ ë¹„êµ

ì•„í‚¤í…ì²˜ì—°ë„í•µì‹¬ ê¸°ë²•íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°íŠ¹ì§•
LeNet-51998Convâ†’Poolâ†’FC60KCNNì˜ ì‹œì´ˆ, ì†ê¸€ì”¨ ì¸ì‹
AlexNet2012ReLU, Dropout, GPU60Më”¥ëŸ¬ë‹ ë¶ì˜ ì‹œì‘
VGGNet20143Ã—3 í•„í„° ë°˜ë³µ138Më‹¨ìˆœí•œ êµ¬ì¡°, ê¹Šì€ ë„¤íŠ¸ì›Œí¬
GoogLeNet2014Inception ëª¨ë“ˆ6.8Më‹¤ì–‘í•œ í•„í„° í¬ê¸° ë³‘ë ¬ ì ìš©
ResNet2015ì”ì°¨ ì—°ê²° (Skip)25M (50)100+ì¸µ í•™ìŠµ ê°€ëŠ¥, ê°€ì¥ ë²”ìš©
DenseNet2017ë°€ì§‘ ì—°ê²°8M (121)ëª¨ë“  ì´ì „ ì¸µê³¼ ì—°ê²°
MobileNet2017Depthwise Separable3.4Mëª¨ë°”ì¼/ì—£ì§€ ë°°í¬ìš© ê²½ëŸ‰í™”
EfficientNet2019ë³µí•© ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¼ë§5.3M (B0)ê¹Šì´Ã—ë„ˆë¹„Ã—í•´ìƒë„ ìµœì  ê· í˜•
ConvNeXt2022Transformer ê¸°ë²• ì ìš©29Mí˜„ëŒ€í™”ëœ ìˆœìˆ˜ CNN, ViT ê²½ìŸ

ë°ì´í„° ì¦ê°• (Data Augmentation)

# Keras â€” ë ˆì´ì–´ ê¸°ë°˜ ì¦ê°• (GPU ê°€ì†, ëª¨ë¸ì— í¬í•¨) data_augmentation = keras.Sequential([ layers.RandomFlip("horizontal"), layers.RandomRotation(0.1), # Â±36ë„ layers.RandomZoom(0.2), # Â±20% í™•ëŒ€/ì¶•ì†Œ layers.RandomTranslation(0.1, 0.1), # Â±10% ì´ë™ layers.RandomContrast(0.2), ]) model = keras.Sequential([ data_augmentation, # í•™ìŠµ ì‹œì—ë§Œ ì ìš© (ì¶”ë¡  ì‹œ ìë™ ë¹„í™œì„±í™”) layers.Conv2D(32, 3, activation="relu"), # ... ]) # PyTorch â€” torchvision.transforms from torchvision import transforms transform_train = transforms.Compose([ transforms.RandomResizedCrop(224, scale=(0.8, 1.0)), transforms.RandomHorizontalFlip(p=0.5), transforms.RandomRotation(15), transforms.ColorJitter(brightness=0.2, contrast=0.2, saturation=0.2, hue=0.1), transforms.RandomErasing(p=0.3), # ëœë¤ ì˜ì—­ ë§ˆìŠ¤í‚¹ (CutOut) transforms.ToTensor(), transforms.Normalize([0.485, 0.456, 0.406], [0.229, 0.224, 0.225]), ]) # albumentations â€” ê³ ê¸‰ ì¦ê°• ë¼ì´ë¸ŒëŸ¬ë¦¬ (pip install albumentations) import albumentations as A from albumentations.pytorch import ToTensorV2 aug = A.Compose([ A.RandomCrop(224, 224), A.HorizontalFlip(p=0.5), A.OneOf([ # ì…‹ ì¤‘ í•˜ë‚˜ë§Œ ì ìš© A.GaussNoise(var_limit=(10, 50)), A.GaussianBlur(blur_limit=3), A.MotionBlur(blur_limit=3), ], p=0.3), A.Normalize(mean=[0.485, 0.456, 0.406], std=[0.229, 0.224, 0.225]), ToTensorV2(), ])
GlobalAveragePooling vs Flatten: Flattenì€ íŠ¹ì„±ë§µì„ 1ì°¨ì›ìœ¼ë¡œ í´ì„œ íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°ê°€ í­ì¦í•˜ê³  ê³¼ì í•© ìœ„í—˜ì´ í½ë‹ˆë‹¤. GlobalAveragePooling2DëŠ” ê° íŠ¹ì„±ë§µì˜ í‰ê· ì„ ë‚´ì–´ íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° ìˆ˜ë¥¼ ëŒ€í­ ì¤„ì´ë©°, í˜„ëŒ€ CNNì—ì„œ í‘œì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

CNN í•µì‹¬ ì •ë¦¬

ê°œë…ì„¤ëª…ê¶Œì¥ ì„¤ì •
ì»¤ë„ í¬ê¸°í•„í„° í¬ê¸°, ì‘ì„ìˆ˜ë¡ ê¹Šì´ë¡œ ë³´ìƒ3Ã—3 (ê°€ì¥ ë²”ìš©)
íŒ¨ë”©ì…ë ¥ í…Œë‘ë¦¬ 0 ì±„ì›€"same" / padding=1 (í¬ê¸° ìœ ì§€)
ìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¼ì´ë“œí•„í„° ì´ë™ ê°„ê²©1 (íŠ¹ì§• ì¶”ì¶œ), 2 (ë‹¤ìš´ìƒ˜í”Œë§)
í’€ë§ê³µê°„ ë‹¤ìš´ìƒ˜í”Œë§MaxPool 2Ã—2 ë˜ëŠ” stride=2 Conv
ì •ê·œí™”í•™ìŠµ ì•ˆì •í™”BatchNorm (Conv ì§í›„)
í™œì„±í™”ë¹„ì„ í˜•ì„± ë„ì…ReLU (ê¸°ë³¸), GELU (Transformerê³„ì—´)
ì¶œë ¥ í’€ë§íŠ¹ì„±ë§µâ†’ë²¡í„° ë³€í™˜GlobalAveragePooling (Flatten ëŒ€ì‹ )
í•„í„° ìˆ˜ íŒ¨í„´ê¹Šì–´ì§ˆìˆ˜ë¡ ì¦ê°€32â†’64â†’128â†’256 (2ë°°ì”©)

RNN/LSTM (ì‹œí€€ìŠ¤ ë°ì´í„°)

ìˆœí™˜ ì‹ ê²½ë§(Recurrent Neural Network)ì€ ì‹œí€€ìŠ¤ ë°ì´í„°(í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸, ì‹œê³„ì—´, ìŒì„±)ë¥¼ ì²˜ë¦¬í•˜ëŠ” ì•„í‚¤í…ì²˜ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. LSTMê³¼ GRUëŠ” ì¥ê¸° ì˜ì¡´ì„± ë¬¸ì œ(ê¸°ìš¸ê¸° ì†Œì‹¤)ë¥¼ í•´ê²°í•œ ë°œì „ëœ RNN ì…€ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.

RNN/LSTM/GRU ë¹„êµ

ì…€ íƒ€ì…ê²Œì´íŠ¸íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°ì¥ì ë‹¨ì 
SimpleRNNì—†ìŒì ìŒê°„ë‹¨, ë¹ ë¦„ê¸°ìš¸ê¸° ì†Œì‹¤ ì‹¬í•¨, ì¥ê¸° ì˜ì¡´ì„± ë¶ˆê°€
LSTMforget, input, output (3ê°œ)ë§ìŒì¥ê¸° ì˜ì¡´ì„± í•™ìŠµ, ê°€ì¥ ë²”ìš©ëŠë¦¼, ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ ì‚¬ìš© ë†’ìŒ
GRUreset, update (2ê°œ)ì¤‘ê°„LSTMê³¼ ìœ ì‚¬ ì„±ëŠ¥, ë” ë¹ ë¦„ë§¤ìš° ê¸´ ì‹œí€€ìŠ¤ì—ì„œ LSTMë³´ë‹¤ ì•½ê°„ ì—´ì„¸

LSTM/GRU â€” Keras êµ¬í˜„

from tensorflow import keras from tensorflow.keras import layers # í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë¶„ë¥˜ (ê°ì • ë¶„ì„) model = keras.Sequential([ layers.Embedding(10000, 128), # ì–´íœ˜ 10000ê°œ â†’ 128ì°¨ì› ë²¡í„° layers.LSTM(128, dropout=0.2), # ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í… ì¶œë ¥ë§Œ ë°˜í™˜ layers.Dense(1, activation="sigmoid") # ì´ì§„ ë¶„ë¥˜ ]) # ì–‘ë°©í–¥ (Bidirectional) â€” ê³¼ê±°+ë¯¸ë˜ ë¬¸ë§¥ ëª¨ë‘ í™œìš© model = keras.Sequential([ layers.Embedding(10000, 128), layers.Bidirectional(layers.LSTM(64)), # ì¶œë ¥ ì°¨ì›: 64Ã—2 = 128 layers.Dense(1, activation="sigmoid") ]) # ë‹¤ì¸µ (Stacked) LSTM â€” return_sequences=Trueë¡œ ëª¨ë“  íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í… ì „ë‹¬ model = keras.Sequential([ layers.Embedding(10000, 128), layers.LSTM(128, return_sequences=True, dropout=0.2), # (batch, seq, 128) layers.LSTM(64, dropout=0.2), # (batch, 64) layers.Dense(1, activation="sigmoid") ]) # GRU â€” LSTMë³´ë‹¤ ê²½ëŸ‰, ë¹„ìŠ·í•œ ì„±ëŠ¥ model = keras.Sequential([ layers.Embedding(10000, 128), layers.GRU(64, return_sequences=True), layers.GRU(32), layers.Dense(1, activation="sigmoid") ]) # ì‹œê³„ì—´ ì˜ˆì¸¡ (Sequence-to-One) model = keras.Sequential([ layers.LSTM(64, input_shape=(30, 5)), # 30 íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í…, 5 íŠ¹ì„± layers.Dense(1) # ë‹¤ìŒ ê°’ ì˜ˆì¸¡ (íšŒê·€) ]) # ì‹œê³„ì—´ ë‹¤ì¤‘ ìŠ¤í… ì˜ˆì¸¡ (Sequence-to-Sequence) model = keras.Sequential([ layers.LSTM(64, return_sequences=True, input_shape=(30, 5)), layers.LSTM(32, return_sequences=True), layers.TimeDistributed(layers.Dense(1)) # ê° íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í…ì— Dense ì ìš© ])

LSTM/GRU â€” PyTorch êµ¬í˜„

import torch import torch.nn as nn class TextClassifier(nn.Module): def __init__(self, vocab_size, embed_dim, hidden_dim, num_classes): super().__init__() self.embedding = nn.Embedding(vocab_size, embed_dim, padding_idx=0) self.lstm = nn.LSTM( embed_dim, hidden_dim, num_layers=2, # 2ì¸µ ìŠ¤íƒ batch_first=True, # ì…ë ¥: (batch, seq, features) bidirectional=True, # ì–‘ë°©í–¥ dropout=0.3, # ì¸µ ê°„ ë“œë¡­ì•„ì›ƒ ) self.fc = nn.Linear(hidden_dim * 2, num_classes) # Ã—2: ì–‘ë°©í–¥ self.dropout = nn.Dropout(0.5) def forward(self, x): embedded = self.embedding(x) # (batch, seq, embed_dim) output, (hidden, cell) = self.lstm(embedded) # hidden: (num_layers*directions, batch, hidden_dim) # ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ì¸µì˜ ì •ë°©í–¥ + ì—­ë°©í–¥ ê²°í•© hidden = torch.cat([hidden[-2], hidden[-1]], dim=1) return self.fc(self.dropout(hidden)) # GRU ë²„ì „ â€” cell state ì—†ìŒ class GRUClassifier(nn.Module): def __init__(self, vocab_size, embed_dim, hidden_dim, num_classes): super().__init__() self.embedding = nn.Embedding(vocab_size, embed_dim) self.gru = nn.GRU(embed_dim, hidden_dim, batch_first=True, bidirectional=True) self.fc = nn.Linear(hidden_dim * 2, num_classes) def forward(self, x): embedded = self.embedding(x) output, hidden = self.gru(embedded) # GRUëŠ” hiddenë§Œ ë°˜í™˜ (cell ì—†ìŒ) hidden = torch.cat([hidden[-2], hidden[-1]], dim=1) return self.fc(hidden) # ì‹œê³„ì—´ ì˜ˆì¸¡ class TimeSeriesLSTM(nn.Module): def __init__(self, input_dim, hidden_dim, output_dim): super().__init__() self.lstm = nn.LSTM(input_dim, hidden_dim, num_layers=2, batch_first=True, dropout=0.2) self.fc = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, output_dim) def forward(self, x): out, _ = self.lstm(x) # (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim) return self.fc(out[:, -1, :]) # ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í…ë§Œ ì‚¬ìš©

íŒ¨ë”© & íŒ¨í‚¹ (ê°€ë³€ ê¸¸ì´ ì‹œí€€ìŠ¤ ì²˜ë¦¬)

# Keras â€” ìë™ íŒ¨ë”©/ë§ˆìŠ¤í‚¹ padded = keras.utils.pad_sequences(sequences, maxlen=200, padding="post") # Embeddingì˜ mask_zero=Trueë¡œ íŒ¨ë”© ìœ„ì¹˜ ìë™ ë¬´ì‹œ layers.Embedding(10000, 128, mask_zero=True) # PyTorch â€” pack_padded_sequence (íš¨ìœ¨ì  ì—°ì‚°) from torch.nn.utils.rnn import pad_sequence, pack_padded_sequence, pad_packed_sequence # ê°€ë³€ ê¸¸ì´ ì‹œí€€ìŠ¤ íŒ¨ë”© sequences = [torch.tensor([1,2,3]), torch.tensor([4,5]), torch.tensor([6])] padded = pad_sequence(sequences, batch_first=True, padding_value=0) # tensor([[1, 2, 3], # [4, 5, 0], # [6, 0, 0]]) lengths = torch.tensor([3, 2, 1]) packed = pack_padded_sequence(padded, lengths, batch_first=True, enforce_sorted=False) output, hidden = lstm(packed) # íŒ¨ë”© ìœ„ì¹˜ ì—°ì‚° ê±´ë„ˆëœ€ output, out_lengths = pad_packed_sequence(output, batch_first=True) # ë‹¤ì‹œ íŒ¨ë”©
ì£¼ì˜: return_sequences=True(Keras) / output(PyTorch)ëŠ” ëª¨ë“  íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í…ì˜ ì¶œë ¥ì„ ë°˜í™˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. ë‹¤ì¸µ RNNì—ì„œ ì¤‘ê°„ ë ˆì´ì–´ëŠ” ë°˜ë“œì‹œ ëª¨ë“  íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í…ì„ ë‹¤ìŒ ë ˆì´ì–´ì— ì „ë‹¬í•´ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. PyTorch LSTMì˜ ê¸°ë³¸ ì…ë ¥ì€ (seq, batch, features)ì´ë©°, batch_first=Trueë¡œ (batch, seq, features)ë¡œ ë³€ê²½í•˜ëŠ” ê²ƒì„ ê¶Œì¥í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

RNN/LSTM í•µì‹¬ ì •ë¦¬

ì‘ì—…ê¶Œì¥ êµ¬ì¡°ë¹„ê³ 
í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë¶„ë¥˜Embedding â†’ BiLSTM â†’ Denseì–‘ë°©í–¥ì´ ë‹¨ë°©í–¥ë³´ë‹¤ ìš°ìˆ˜
ê°ì„± ë¶„ì„Embedding â†’ BiGRU â†’ DenseGRUê°€ ë” ë¹ ë¥´ê³  ë¹„ìŠ·í•œ ì„±ëŠ¥
ì‹œê³„ì—´ ì˜ˆì¸¡ (ë‹¨ì¼)LSTM â†’ Dense(1)ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í… ì‚¬ìš©
ì‹œê³„ì—´ ì˜ˆì¸¡ (ë‹¤ì¤‘)LSTM(return_seq) â†’ TimeDistributedëª¨ë“  íƒ€ì„ìŠ¤í… ì˜ˆì¸¡
ê¸°ê³„ ë²ˆì—­Encoder-Decoder + AttentionTransformerë¡œ ëŒ€ì²´ ì¶”ì„¸
ìŒì„± ì¸ì‹BiLSTM + CTC Lossê°€ë³€ ê¸¸ì´ ì •ë ¬ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”
ì¼ë°˜ ê¶Œì¥Transformerê¸´ ì‹œí€€ìŠ¤, ë³‘ë ¬í™” ìš°ìˆ˜

Transformer (ìì—°ì–´ ì²˜ë¦¬)

TransformerëŠ” Self-Attention ë©”ì»¤ë‹ˆì¦˜ ê¸°ë°˜ìœ¼ë¡œ ì‹œí€€ìŠ¤ë¥¼ ë³‘ë ¬ ì²˜ë¦¬í•˜ëŠ” ì•„í‚¤í…ì²˜ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. RNNì˜ ìˆœì°¨ ì²˜ë¦¬ í•œê³„ë¥¼ ê·¹ë³µí•˜ì—¬ NLP(BERT, GPT), ë¹„ì „(ViT), ìŒì„± ë“± ê±°ì˜ ëª¨ë“  ë¶„ì•¼ì—ì„œ ìµœê³  ì„±ëŠ¥ì„ ë‹¬ì„±í•˜ê³  ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. "Attention Is All You Need" (2017) ë…¼ë¬¸ì—ì„œ ì œì•ˆë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

Self-Attention ë©”ì»¤ë‹ˆì¦˜

# Scaled Dot-Product Attention # # Attention(Q, K, V) = softmax(QÂ·K^T / âˆšd_k) Â· V # # Q (Query) : "ë‚´ê°€ ì°¾ëŠ” ê²ƒ" â€” ê° í† í°ì´ ë‹¤ë¥¸ í† í°ì—ê²Œ ë¬»ëŠ” ì§ˆì˜ # K (Key) : "ë‚´ê°€ ê°€ì§„ ê²ƒ" â€” ê° í† í°ì´ ì œê³µí•˜ëŠ” í‚¤ # V (Value) : "ë‚´ ë‚´ìš©" â€” ì‹¤ì œ ì „ë‹¬í•  ì •ë³´ # âˆšd_k : ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¼ë§ â€” ë‚´ì  ê°’ì´ ì»¤ì§€ë©´ softmax ê¸°ìš¸ê¸° ì†Œì‹¤ ë°©ì§€ import torch import torch.nn as nn import torch.nn.functional as F import math def scaled_dot_product_attention(Q, K, V, mask=None): d_k = Q.size(-1) scores = torch.matmul(Q, K.transpose(-2, -1)) / math.sqrt(d_k) # (batch, heads, seq, seq) if mask is not None: scores = scores.masked_fill(mask == 0, float("-inf")) # ë§ˆìŠ¤í‚¹ ìœ„ì¹˜ -âˆ attn_weights = F.softmax(scores, dim=-1) # ì–´í…ì…˜ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ output = torch.matmul(attn_weights, V) # ê°€ì¤‘ í•© return output, attn_weights

Multi-Head Attention (PyTorch êµ¬í˜„)

class MultiHeadAttention(nn.Module): def __init__(self, d_model, num_heads): super().__init__() assert d_model % num_heads == 0 self.d_model = d_model self.num_heads = num_heads self.d_k = d_model // num_heads self.W_q = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model) self.W_k = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model) self.W_v = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model) self.W_o = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model) def forward(self, query, key, value, mask=None): batch_size = query.size(0) # ì„ í˜• ë³€í™˜ í›„ í—¤ë“œ ë¶„í• : (batch, seq, d_model) â†’ (batch, heads, seq, d_k) Q = self.W_q(query).view(batch_size, -1, self.num_heads, self.d_k).transpose(1, 2) K = self.W_k(key).view(batch_size, -1, self.num_heads, self.d_k).transpose(1, 2) V = self.W_v(value).view(batch_size, -1, self.num_heads, self.d_k).transpose(1, 2) # Scaled Dot-Product Attention attn_out, attn_weights = scaled_dot_product_attention(Q, K, V, mask) # í—¤ë“œ ê²°í•©: (batch, heads, seq, d_k) â†’ (batch, seq, d_model) attn_out = attn_out.transpose(1, 2).contiguous().view(batch_size, -1, self.d_model) return self.W_o(attn_out) # PyTorch ë‚´ì¥ (ê¶Œì¥ â€” Flash Attention ìë™ ì ìš©) mha = nn.MultiheadAttention(embed_dim=512, num_heads=8, batch_first=True) attn_output, attn_weights = mha(query, key, value, attn_mask=mask)

Positional Encoding

# TransformerëŠ” ìœ„ì¹˜ ì •ë³´ê°€ ì—†ìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ Positional Encodingì„ ì¶”ê°€ # PE(pos, 2i) = sin(pos / 10000^(2i/d_model)) # PE(pos, 2i+1) = cos(pos / 10000^(2i/d_model)) class PositionalEncoding(nn.Module): def __init__(self, d_model, max_len=5000, dropout=0.1): super().__init__() self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout) pe = torch.zeros(max_len, d_model) position = torch.arange(0, max_len).unsqueeze(1).float() div_term = torch.exp(torch.arange(0, d_model, 2).float() * -(math.log(10000.0) / d_model)) pe[:, 0::2] = torch.sin(position * div_term) # ì§ìˆ˜ ì¸ë±ìŠ¤: sin pe[:, 1::2] = torch.cos(position * div_term) # í™€ìˆ˜ ì¸ë±ìŠ¤: cos pe = pe.unsqueeze(0) # (1, max_len, d_model) self.register_buffer("pe", pe) def forward(self, x): x = x + self.pe[:, :x.size(1)] return self.dropout(x)

Transformer Encoder Block

class TransformerEncoderBlock(nn.Module): def __init__(self, d_model, num_heads, d_ff, dropout=0.1): super().__init__() self.self_attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(d_model, num_heads, batch_first=True) self.ffn = nn.Sequential( nn.Linear(d_model, d_ff), # d_ff = d_model Ã— 4 ê°€ ì¼ë°˜ì  nn.GELU(), nn.Dropout(dropout), nn.Linear(d_ff, d_model), ) self.norm1 = nn.LayerNorm(d_model) self.norm2 = nn.LayerNorm(d_model) self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout) def forward(self, x, mask=None): # Pre-LayerNorm êµ¬ì¡° (Post-LNë³´ë‹¤ í•™ìŠµ ì•ˆì •ì ) normed = self.norm1(x) attn_out, _ = self.self_attn(normed, normed, normed, attn_mask=mask) x = x + self.dropout(attn_out) # ì”ì°¨ ì—°ê²° normed = self.norm2(x) ffn_out = self.ffn(normed) x = x + self.dropout(ffn_out) # ì”ì°¨ ì—°ê²° return x # PyTorch ë‚´ì¥ Encoder (ê¶Œì¥) encoder_layer = nn.TransformerEncoderLayer( d_model=512, nhead=8, dim_feedforward=2048, dropout=0.1, activation="gelu", batch_first=True, norm_first=True ) encoder = nn.TransformerEncoder(encoder_layer, num_layers=6)

Transformer Decoder Block

class TransformerDecoderBlock(nn.Module): def __init__(self, d_model, num_heads, d_ff, dropout=0.1): super().__init__() self.self_attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(d_model, num_heads, batch_first=True) self.cross_attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(d_model, num_heads, batch_first=True) self.ffn = nn.Sequential( nn.Linear(d_model, d_ff), nn.GELU(), nn.Dropout(dropout), nn.Linear(d_ff, d_model), ) self.norm1 = nn.LayerNorm(d_model) self.norm2 = nn.LayerNorm(d_model) self.norm3 = nn.LayerNorm(d_model) self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout) def forward(self, x, encoder_out, tgt_mask=None, memory_mask=None): # â‘  Masked Self-Attention (ë¯¸ë˜ í† í° ì°¸ì¡° ë°©ì§€) normed = self.norm1(x) attn_out, _ = self.self_attn(normed, normed, normed, attn_mask=tgt_mask) x = x + self.dropout(attn_out) # â‘¡ Cross-Attention (ì¸ì½”ë” ì¶œë ¥ ì°¸ì¡°) normed = self.norm2(x) attn_out, _ = self.cross_attn(normed, encoder_out, encoder_out, attn_mask=memory_mask) x = x + self.dropout(attn_out) # â‘¢ Feed-Forward normed = self.norm3(x) x = x + self.dropout(self.ffn(normed)) return x # Causal Mask ìƒì„± (ë””ì½”ë”ìš© â€” ë¯¸ë˜ í† í° ê°€ë¦¬ê¸°) def generate_causal_mask(seq_len): return torch.triu(torch.ones(seq_len, seq_len), diagonal=1).bool() # [[False, True, True ], # [False, False, True ], # [False, False, False]]

ì™„ì „í•œ Transformer ëª¨ë¸ (ë¶„ë¥˜)

class TransformerClassifier(nn.Module): def __init__(self, vocab_size, d_model=256, num_heads=8, num_layers=4, d_ff=512, num_classes=2, max_len=512, dropout=0.1): super().__init__() self.embedding = nn.Embedding(vocab_size, d_model) self.pos_encoding = PositionalEncoding(d_model, max_len, dropout) encoder_layer = nn.TransformerEncoderLayer( d_model, num_heads, d_ff, dropout, activation="gelu", batch_first=True, norm_first=True ) self.encoder = nn.TransformerEncoder(encoder_layer, num_layers) self.classifier = nn.Sequential( nn.LayerNorm(d_model), nn.Linear(d_model, num_classes) ) def forward(self, x, src_mask=None): x = self.embedding(x) * math.sqrt(self.d_model) # ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¼ë§ x = self.pos_encoding(x) x = self.encoder(x, src_key_padding_mask=src_mask) x = x.mean(dim=1) # í‰ê·  í’€ë§ (ë˜ëŠ” [CLS] í† í°) return self.classifier(x)

Hugging Face Transformers í™œìš©

# pip install transformers datasets # â‘  Pipeline â€” ê°€ì¥ ê°„ë‹¨í•œ ì‚¬ìš©ë²• (ì¶”ë¡  ì „ìš©) from transformers import pipeline # ê°ì„± ë¶„ì„ classifier = pipeline("sentiment-analysis") result = classifier("This movie is amazing!") # [{'label': 'POSITIVE', 'score': 0.9998}] # í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìƒì„± generator = pipeline("text-generation", model="gpt2") output = generator("The future of AI", max_length=50) # ì§ˆì˜ì‘ë‹µ qa = pipeline("question-answering") result = qa(question="What is PyTorch?", context="PyTorch is a deep learning framework.") # ìš”ì•½ summarizer = pipeline("summarization", model="facebook/bart-large-cnn") summary = summarizer(long_text, max_length=130, min_length=30) # â‘¡ ì§ì ‘ ëª¨ë¸ ë¡œë“œ â€” í† í¬ë‚˜ì´ì € + ëª¨ë¸ from transformers import AutoTokenizer, AutoModel, AutoModelForSequenceClassification tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained("bert-base-uncased") model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained("bert-base-uncased", num_labels=2) # í† í¬ë‚˜ì´ì§• inputs = tokenizer( "Hello, how are you?", padding=True, truncation=True, max_length=128, return_tensors="pt" # "pt"=PyTorch, "tf"=TensorFlow, "np"=NumPy ) # {'input_ids': tensor([[101, 7592, ...]]), 'attention_mask': tensor([[1, 1, ...]])} outputs = model(**inputs) logits = outputs.logits # (batch, num_labels) # â‘¢ íŒŒì¸íŠœë‹ (Hugging Face Trainer) from transformers import TrainingArguments, Trainer from datasets import load_dataset dataset = load_dataset("imdb") def tokenize_fn(examples): return tokenizer(examples["text"], truncation=True, max_length=256) tokenized = dataset.map(tokenize_fn, batched=True) training_args = TrainingArguments( output_dir="./results", num_train_epochs=3, per_device_train_batch_size=16, per_device_eval_batch_size=64, learning_rate=2e-5, weight_decay=0.01, eval_strategy="epoch", save_strategy="epoch", load_best_model_at_end=True, fp16=True, # í˜¼í•© ì •ë°€ë„ ) trainer = Trainer( model=model, args=training_args, train_dataset=tokenized["train"], eval_dataset=tokenized["test"], ) trainer.train()

ì£¼ìš” Transformer ëª¨ë¸ ë¹„êµ

ëª¨ë¸êµ¬ì¡°íŠ¹ì§•ì£¼ìš” ìš©ë„

T5Encoder-Decoderëª¨ë“  NLPë¥¼ text-to-textë¡œ í†µí•©ë²ˆì—­, ìš”ì•½, QA
BARTEncoder-Decoderë…¸ì´ì¦ˆ ì œê±° ìê¸°ë¶€í˜¸í™”ê¸°ìš”ì•½, ë²ˆì—­

ViTEncoderì´ë¯¸ì§€ë¥¼ íŒ¨ì¹˜ë¡œ ë¶„í• í•˜ì—¬ ì²˜ë¦¬ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ë¶„ë¥˜
WhisperEncoder-DecoderìŒì„±â†’í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë²”ìš© ëª¨ë¸ìŒì„± ì¸ì‹, ë²ˆì—­
LLaMADecoderíš¨ìœ¨ì  ì˜¤í”ˆì†ŒìŠ¤ LLMí…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìƒì„±, ì¶”ë¡ 
Transformer í•˜ì´í¼íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„° ê°€ì´ë“œ: d_model = ì„ë² ë”© ì°¨ì› (256~1024), num_heads = ì–´í…ì…˜ í—¤ë“œ ìˆ˜ (d_modelì˜ ì•½ìˆ˜, ë³´í†µ 8~16), d_ff = FFN íˆë“  ì°¨ì› (ë³´í†µ d_model Ã— 4), num_layers = ë¸”ë¡ ìˆ˜ (6~12). í•™ìŠµë¥ ì€ ì›Œë°ì—…(warmup) í›„ ê°ì†Œí•˜ëŠ” ìŠ¤ì¼€ì¤„ì´ í•„ìˆ˜ì ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.

Transformer í•µì‹¬ ì •ë¦¬

êµ¬ì„± ìš”ì†Œì—­í• í•µì‹¬ í¬ì¸íŠ¸
Self-Attentioní† í° ê°„ ê´€ê³„ ëª¨ë¸ë§O(nÂ²) ë³µì¡ë„, Flash Attentionìœ¼ë¡œ ê°œì„ 
Multi-Headë‹¤ì–‘í•œ ê´€ê³„ íŒ¨í„´ í¬ì°©í—¤ë“œë³„ ë…ë¦½ ì–´í…ì…˜ í›„ ê²°í•©
Positional Encodingìˆœì„œ ì •ë³´ ë¶€ì—¬sin/cos (ê³ ì •) ë˜ëŠ” í•™ìŠµ ê°€ëŠ¥
Feed-Forwardë¹„ì„ í˜• ë³€í™˜ê° ìœ„ì¹˜ì— ë…ë¦½ ì ìš© (MLP)
LayerNormí•™ìŠµ ì•ˆì •í™”Pre-LN (ë¸”ë¡ ì•) ì´ ë” ì•ˆì •ì 
ì”ì°¨ ì—°ê²°ê·¸ë˜ë””ì–¸íŠ¸ íë¦„ ë³´ì¡´ëª¨ë“  ì„œë¸Œë ˆì´ì–´ì— ì ìš©
Causal Maskë¯¸ë˜ í† í° ê°€ë¦¬ê¸°ë””ì½”ë”/ìê¸°íšŒê·€ ëª¨ë¸ í•„ìˆ˜
Cross-Attentionì¸ì½”ë”-ë””ì½”ë” ì—°ê²°Q=ë””ì½”ë”, K/V=ì¸ì½”ë”

ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ (Transfer Learning)

ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµì€ ëŒ€ê·œëª¨ ë°ì´í„°ë¡œ ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµëœ ëª¨ë¸ì˜ ì§€ì‹ì„ ìƒˆë¡œìš´ ì‘ì—…ì— ì¬í™œìš©í•˜ëŠ” ê¸°ë²•ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. ì ì€ ë°ì´í„°ì™€ ì§§ì€ í•™ìŠµ ì‹œê°„ìœ¼ë¡œ ë†’ì€ ì„±ëŠ¥ì„ ë‹¬ì„±í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆì–´, ì‹¤ë¬´ì—ì„œ ëª¨ë¸ì„ ì²˜ìŒë¶€í„° í•™ìŠµí•˜ëŠ” ê²½ìš°ë³´ë‹¤ ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ëŠ” ê²½ìš°ê°€ í›¨ì”¬ ë” ë§ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ ì „ëµ

ì „ëµë°©ë²•ë°ì´í„° ì–‘ì í•©í•œ ê²½ìš°
Feature Extractionì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ë ˆì´ì–´ ë™ê²°, í—¤ë“œë§Œ í•™ìŠµì ìŒ (<1000)ìƒˆ ë°ì´í„°ê°€ ì›ë³¸ê³¼ ìœ ì‚¬
Fine-tuning (ì „ì²´)ëª¨ë“  ë ˆì´ì–´ë¥¼ ë‚®ì€ lrë¡œ í•™ìŠµë§ìŒ (>10000)ë°ì´í„° ì¶©ë¶„, ë„ë©”ì¸ ë‹¤ë¦„
Gradual Unfreezingë’¤ìª½ ë ˆì´ì–´ë¶€í„° ìˆœì°¨ì  í•´ë™ì¤‘ê°„ì•ˆì •ì ì¸ íŒŒì¸íŠœë‹
Discriminative LRë ˆì´ì–´ë³„ ë‹¤ë¥¸ í•™ìŠµë¥ ì¤‘ê°„~ë§ìŒì•ìª½=ë‚®ì€lr, ë’¤ìª½=ë†’ì€lr

ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ â€” Keras

from tensorflow import keras from tensorflow.keras import layers from tensorflow.keras.applications import EfficientNetV2B0, ResNet50V2 # â‘  Feature Extraction (íŠ¹ì„± ì¶”ì¶œ) â€” ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ë ˆì´ì–´ ë™ê²° base_model = EfficientNetV2B0(weights="imagenet", include_top=False, input_shape=(224, 224, 3)) base_model.trainable = False # ëª¨ë“  ë ˆì´ì–´ ë™ê²° model = keras.Sequential([ base_model, layers.GlobalAveragePooling2D(), layers.Dropout(0.3), layers.Dense(128, activation="relu"), layers.Dense(10, activation="softmax") ]) model.compile(optimizer=keras.optimizers.Adam(1e-3), # ë†’ì€ lr OK (í—¤ë“œë§Œ í•™ìŠµ) loss="sparse_categorical_crossentropy", metrics=["accuracy"]) model.fit(train_ds, epochs=10, validation_data=val_ds) # â‘¡ Fine-tuning â€” í—¤ë“œ í•™ìŠµ í›„ ì¼ë¶€ ë ˆì´ì–´ í•´ë™ base_model.trainable = True for layer in base_model.layers[:-30]: # ì•ìª½ ë ˆì´ì–´ëŠ” ë™ê²° ìœ ì§€ layer.trainable = False model.compile(optimizer=keras.optimizers.Adam(1e-5), # ë§¤ìš° ë‚®ì€ lr (ê¸°ì¡´ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ ë³´í˜¸) loss="sparse_categorical_crossentropy", metrics=["accuracy"]) model.fit(train_ds, epochs=10, validation_data=val_ds) # ì‚¬ìš© ê°€ëŠ¥í•œ ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ëª¨ë¸ # keras.applications.EfficientNetV2B0~L â€” íš¨ìœ¨ì , ìµœì‹  ê¶Œì¥ # keras.applications.ResNet50V2 â€” ë²”ìš©, ê²€ì¦ëœ ì„±ëŠ¥ # keras.applications.MobileNetV3Large â€” ëª¨ë°”ì¼/ì—£ì§€ìš© # keras.applications.ConvNeXtTiny â€” ìµœì‹  ìˆœìˆ˜ CNN

ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ â€” PyTorch

import torch import torch.nn as nn from torchvision import models # â‘  Feature Extraction model = models.efficientnet_v2_s(weights="IMAGENET1K_V1") # ëª¨ë“  ë ˆì´ì–´ ë™ê²° for param in model.parameters(): param.requires_grad = False # ë¶„ë¥˜ í—¤ë“œ êµì²´ model.classifier = nn.Sequential( nn.Dropout(0.3), nn.Linear(model.classifier[1].in_features, 10) ) # êµì²´ëœ í—¤ë“œë§Œ í•™ìŠµë¨ (requires_grad=True ê¸°ë³¸) optimizer = torch.optim.Adam(model.classifier.parameters(), lr=1e-3) # â‘¡ Fine-tuning â€” Discriminative Learning Rate for param in model.parameters(): param.requires_grad = True # ì „ì²´ í•´ë™ optimizer = torch.optim.AdamW([ {"params": model.features[:5].parameters(), "lr": 1e-6}, # ì•ìª½: ì•„ì£¼ ë‚®ì€ lr {"params": model.features[5:].parameters(), "lr": 1e-5}, # ì¤‘ê°„: ë‚®ì€ lr {"params": model.classifier.parameters(), "lr": 1e-3}, # í—¤ë“œ: ë†’ì€ lr ], weight_decay=0.01) # ResNet í—¤ë“œ êµì²´ resnet = models.resnet50(weights="IMAGENET1K_V2") resnet.fc = nn.Linear(resnet.fc.in_features, 10) # ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ FC êµì²´ # ViT (Vision Transformer) ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ vit = models.vit_b_16(weights="IMAGENET1K_V1") vit.heads = nn.Linear(vit.heads[0].in_features, 10)

NLP ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ â€” Hugging Face

from transformers import AutoTokenizer, AutoModelForSequenceClassification # ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ëª¨ë¸ + ë¶„ë¥˜ í—¤ë“œ model_name = "bert-base-uncased" tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name) model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained(model_name, num_labels=3) # Layer-wise Learning Rate Decay (LLRD) from transformers import AdamW no_decay = ["bias", "LayerNorm.weight"] optimizer_grouped = [] lr = 2e-5 decay_rate = 0.9 for i in range(12, -1, -1): # BERT 12ì¸µ â†’ 0ì¸µ layer_lr = lr * (decay_rate ** (12 - i)) layer_params = [(n, p) for n, p in model.named_parameters() if f"layer.{i}." in n] optimizer_grouped.append({ "params": [p for n, p in layer_params if not any(nd in n for nd in no_decay)], "lr": layer_lr, "weight_decay": 0.01 }) # í•œêµ­ì–´ ëª¨ë¸ ì˜ˆì‹œ # tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained("klue/bert-base") # model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained("klue/bert-base", num_labels=5)

ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ëª¨ë¸ ë¹„êµ (ì´ë¯¸ì§€)

ëª¨ë¸íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°ImageNet Top-1ì¶”ë¡  ì†ë„ì í•©í•œ ìš©ë„

ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ ì£¼ì˜ì‚¬í•­: Feature extraction ë‹¨ê³„ì—ì„œëŠ” ë†’ì€ í•™ìŠµë¥ (1e-3)ì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•´ë„ ë˜ì§€ë§Œ, fine-tuning ë‹¨ê³„ì—ì„œëŠ” ë°˜ë“œì‹œ ë‚®ì€ í•™ìŠµë¥ (1e-5~1e-4)ì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì„¸ìš” â€” ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜ê°€ íŒŒê´´ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤. ì…ë ¥ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ì˜ ì „ì²˜ë¦¬(ì •ê·œí™” ê°’)ëŠ” ì‚¬ì „í•™ìŠµ ì‹œ ì‚¬ìš©ëœ ê²ƒê³¼ ë™ì¼í•´ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. ë°ì´í„°ê°€ ë§¤ìš° ì ìœ¼ë©´(<500) fine-tuning ëŒ€ì‹  feature extractionë§Œ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì„¸ìš”.

ì „ì´ í•™ìŠµ í•µì‹¬ ì •ë¦¬

ë‹¨ê³„ë™ê²° ë²”ìœ„í•™ìŠµë¥ ì—í¬í¬

itertools ì˜ˆì œ

from itertools import chain, combinations, permutations, accumulate # ì²´ì¸ list(chain([1,2], [3,4])) # [1,2,3,4] # ìˆœì—´ list(permutations("ABC", 2)) # [('A','B'), ('A','C'), ...] # ì¡°í•© list(combinations("ABC", 2)) # [('A','B'), ('A','C'), ('B','C')] # ëˆ„ì  list(accumulate([1,2,3,4])) # [1, 3, 6, 10]

from functools import lru_cache, partial, reduce # ë©”ëª¨ì´ì œì´ì…˜ @lru_cache def fib(n): if n < 2: return n return fib(n-1) + fib(n-2) # ë¶€ë¶„ í•¨ìˆ˜ add5 = partial(lambda x, y: x + y, 5) add5(3) # 8 # ëˆ„ì  ê³„ì‚° reduce(lambda x, y: x + y, [1,2,3,4]) # 10
